# Policy Statement:
#
# In accordance with RFC5892, the following code points have additional
# contextual rules. Any IDN label containing one of the characters listed
# below MUST also include at least one character from the Katakana, Hiragana,
# or Han scripts:
# 
# * U+30FB (KATAKANA MIDDLE DOT)
# * U+3006 (IDEOGRAPHIC CLOSING MARK)
# * U+30FC (KATAKANA-HIRAGANA PROLONGED SOUND MARK)
#
